# Marker Sweep тАФ 2026-07-16 (scutemob-88)

Campaign-wide audit of every non-`Complete` `CardDefinition.completeness` marker
against the **current** engine. Motivated by AC8 and AC9, whose backfills each hit a
stale-marker HIGH (Reforge the Soul was the second consecutive); both workers
recommended this sweep.

**Audited: 742 markers** (68 inert / 626 partial / 47 known-wrong).

## Method

Each marker was audited against three sources: the **capability inventory**
(generated from `crates/card-types/src` тАФ the current variant set), the **def source**,
and the **oracle text** looked up via MCP (a def's own `oracle_text:` field is not
authoritative and was found wrong in at least one case).

The decisive rule, from this project's own `feedback_verify_full_chain`: **a variant
existing is not proof a blocker is stale.** A `TriggerCondition` is only usable if it
*also* has a builder arm in `enrich_spec_from_def` and a dispatch in `check_triggers`;
filter fields exist that `matches_filter` silently ignores. Every `stale-blocker-shipped`
call required tracing the chain and citing file:line for each link.

### Calibration case тАФ Megrim

`megrim.rs` was marked `partial`: *"Requires TriggerCondition::WheneverOpponentDiscards
which does not exist in the DSL тАж Omitted per W5 policy."* Every clause of that note is
false тАФ the variant exists (`card_definition.rs:3287`), the builder arm exists
(`replay_harness.rs:3176`), the event dispatches, and the def **already uses it**. But
Megrim is still not `Complete`: it models *"deals 2 damage"* as `Effect::LoseLife`, and
life loss is not damage (CR 119.3). A sweep that reasoned "note is false тЖТ upgrade"
would have shipped a broken card. The bar for `upgrade-to-complete` was therefore set at
clause-by-clause evidence with high confidence; uncertainty is never an upgrade.

## Results

| Category | Count | Meaning |
|---|---:|---|
| `still-valid` | 434 | stated blocker is real and still missing |
| `stale-blocker-shipped` | 208 | note cites a capability that now exists |
| `wrong-or-vague-note` | 100 | note is vague, contradicted by the def, or the marker kind is wrong |

| Disposition | Count |
|---|---:|
| `keep` | 402 |
| `upgrade-to-complete` | 13 |
| `needs-rewiring` | 117 |
| `rewrite-note` | 156 |
| `fix-marker-kind` | 54 |

**42% of markers (308/742) were wrong in some way** тАФ stale, misleading, or attached to the wrong marker kind. That is the finding: the marker corpus had drifted materially from the engine, exactly as AC8/AC9 suspected.

## Stale тАФ blocker has shipped (208)

The note cites a primitive/capability that now exists. `upgrade-to-complete` = the def already implements the whole card and the marker is pure lag. `needs-rewiring` = the capability exists but the def never used it тАФ real authoring work, **not done here** (see the worklist).

| Card | File | Kind | Disposition | Blocker | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Abstergo Entertainment | `abstergo_entertainment.rs` | `partial` | `rewrite-note` | historic TargetFilter predicate + exile-all-graveyards effect | The inline TODO lists three gaps; one is stale. Cost::ExileSelf EXISTS and is wired (replay_harness.rs:3773 -> ac.exile_self; effects/mod.rs:7631). 'Return up to one target card from your graveyard' is also expressible (TargetRequirement::UpToN + TargetCardInYourGraveyard + MoveZone). But two gaps are REAL: (1) TargetFilter has no historic predicate тАФ the only Historic in the DSL is SpellCostFilter::Historic (card_definition.rs:4123), which is a cost-modifier filter, not a target filter; (2) 'exile all graveyards' is NOT expressible тАФ Effect::ExileAll takes a TargetFilter and only scans obj.zone == ZoneId::Battlefield (effects/mod.rs:1547-1554); EffectFilter::AllCardsInGraveyards is a continuous-effect/layer filter (layers.rs:606) and is not reachable from ExileAll. Card stays partial; rewrite the note so a worker is not sent at the exile-self wall. |
| Access Denied | `access_denied.rs` | `inert` | `needs-rewiring` | STALE: variable token count / ManaValueOf | Note says 'Stripped until MV-tracking + variable token count is in DSL'. Both shipped: TokenSpec.count is an EffectAmount (card_definition.rs:3687) and EffectAmount::ManaValueOf(EffectTarget) exists (:2493), resolving via state.fizzle_object so the countered spell's MV is still readable after it hits the graveyard (effects/mod.rs:6686). Authorable as Sequence[CounterSpell(DeclaredTarget 0), CreateToken{count: ManaValueOf(DeclaredTarget 0)}]. |
| Alexios, Deimos of Kosmos | `alexios_deimos_of_kosmos.rs` | `partial` | `needs-rewiring` | each-player's-upkeep (ambient) trigger scope | The note leads with two shipped primitives: GameRestriction::CantBeSacrificed and GameRestriction::CantAttackOwner both exist (PB-AC8) and AbilityDefinition::StaticRestriction is the carrier тАФ the def has neither wired (abilities ends at MustAttackEachCombat, line 30). That is real authoring work. But the card stays partial afterwards: the upkeep clause is genuinely blocked тАФ TriggerCondition has AtBeginningOfEachUpkeep, yet 'THAT PLAYER gains control' needs the upkeep player as the GainControl recipient, and PlayerTarget has no active/upkeep-player variant (TriggeringPlayer is set from PendingTrigger::triggering_player on discard/draw triggers, not turn-based upkeep events). Do not upgrade. |
| Anafenza, Unyielding Lineage | `anafenza_unyielding_lineage.rs` | `partial` | `needs-rewiring` | Endure keyword action | Note's first claim ('WhenDies with nontoken + controller filter not in DSL') is FALSE. Chain traced: TriggeredAbilityDef.death_filter carries controller_you (abilities.rs:4388), exclude_self (4396) and nontoken_only (4400), all dispatched off TriggerEvent::AnyCreatureDies in check_triggers. Oracle 'Whenever another nontoken creature you control dies' is fully expressible today. Residual: Endure 2 (choose: two +1/+1 counters on Anafenza OR create a 2/2 white Spirit token) тАФ Effect::Choose exists (card_definition.rs:1696) so this is likely authorable, but no card def currently uses Choose for a non-mana modal at resolution, so verify before authoring. Def has abilities: vec![] for the trigger тАФ not close to Complete. |
| Ancient Tomb | `ancient_tomb.rs` | `known_wrong` | `upgrade-to-complete` | none тАФ marker is false | The marker's factual claim is false. Oracle has one clause: '{T}: Add {C}{C}. Ancient Tomb deals 2 damage to you.' The def's shape тАФ Cost::Tap + Effect::Sequence([AddMana, DealDamage{Controller, Fixed(2)}]) тАФ is matched EXACTLY by the pain-land arm of try_as_tap_mana_ability (replay_harness.rs:3680-3693), which returns a ManaAbility with damage_to_controller=2; enrich_spec_from_def then explicitly EXCLUDES it from the activated-ability list because 'These are registered as ManaAbility above via try_as_tap_mana_ability' (replay_harness.rs:2138-2149). The damage is applied inside mana-ability resolution, not on the stack (rules/mana.rs:299-308, comment cites CR 605). So it is a mana ability: opponents cannot respond and it IS usable while casting тАФ the opposite of what the marker says. Calibration: caves_of_koilos.rs uses the identical Sequence([AddMana, DealDamage]) pattern (lines 28-37, 47-56) and carries NO completeness marker (= Complete). mana_pool(0,0,0,0,0,2) is WUBRGC = 2 colorless, correct. Type line Land, mana_cost None, correct. ENGINE-FINDING: rules/mana.rs:303 applies pain-land damage as a raw `player_state.life_total -= n` and emits GameEvent::DamageDealt without routing through the damage replacement/prevention pipeline (CR 615), so prevention shields and damage replacement do not see it. This affects every pain land using this pattern (caves_of_koilos et al.), is engine-wide rather than def-specific, and does not block this marker flip. |

Full chain verified: AbilityDefinition::Activated carries `activation_condition: Option<Condition>`; it is enforced at rules/abilities.rs:254-261 under the comment 'CR 602.5b: "Activate only if [condition]" тАФ check activation condition'; Condition::HasCitysBlessing exists and the def already uses it (line 37, inside a Conditional effect instead); and 15+ defs use the pattern live (temple_of_the_false_god.rs:24, idol_of_oblivion.rs:24, bloodsoaked_champion.rs:31, glistening_sphere.rs:48, shifting_woodland.rs:61, ...). Current def lets a player pay {5}+{T} without the blessing and draw nothing тАФ real wrong game state. Fix is mechanical: set `activation_condition: Some(Condition::HasCitysBlessing)` on the third ability and unwrap the Conditional to a bare DrawCards. |

| Chandra, Flamecaller | `chandra_flamecaller.rs` | `partial` | `needs-rewiring` | Effect::WheelHand / EffectAmount::HandSize (note claims missing; both exist) | The note says 'EffectAmount::HandSize not in DSL'. It IS in the DSL тАФ card_definition.rs:2727, discriminant 21, added by PB-AC3. More directly, Effect::WheelHand { player, disposal, draw } (card_definition.rs:2366-2374) is purpose-built for this shape and its doc even explains why the naive DiscardCards{HandSize}+DrawCards{HandSize} draws 0: the count must be snapshotted before disposal. The 0 ability currently resolves as Effect::Nothing (chandra_flamecaller.rs:46). Rewiring: WheelHand { player: Controller, disposal: WheelDisposal::Discard, draw: WheelDraw::ThatMany } followed by DrawCards(Fixed(1)) for the 'plus one' тАФ WheelDraw has only ThatMany and Fixed (2401-2408), no ThatMany+N, so the author must confirm the split-draw is acceptable (CR 121.3 makes drawing N+1 a sequence of individual draws anyway). ## Wrong or vague note (100)

The note does not describe a real, actionable blocker: too vague, contradicted by the def body, or the marker kind understates the defect. `fix-marker-kind` usually means a `partial` that is really `known_wrong` тАФ the card ships wrong game state, it does not merely omit a clause.

So oracle's 'that player creates a 2/2 black Zombie' puts every token under ACERERAK'S controller тАФ a legal-but-wrong multiplayer bug that hands the Acererak player N free blockers instead of giving each opponent one. Note's inline claim 'Using CdaPowerToughness stub' is misleading тАФ there is no CdaPowerToughness in the abilities list at all, so P/T is simply absent (a 0/0 that would die to SBA); worth correcting when the primitive lands, but the marker and the blocker are both right. |

Correctly left as abilities: vec![] per W5 policy тАФ DoubleTokens would be materially wrong (2N vs N+1 diverges at N>=2). |
| Yuriko, the Tiger's Shadow | `yuriko_the_tigers_shadow.rs` | `partial` | `keep` | No EffectTarget for the card revealed by RevealAndRoute | Still missing, and the note is precise. EffectAmount::ManaValueOf(EffectTarget) does exist (card_definition.rs:2493), but EffectTarget's 11 variants (DeclaredTarget, Controller, EachPlayer, EachOpponent, AllCreatures, AllPermanents, AllPermanentsMatching, Source, LastCreatedPermanent, TriggeringCreature, EquippedCreature) contain nothing that designates the card just revealed by Effect::RevealAndRoute, and no ctx field carries it (EffectContext has last_created_permanent / last_effect_count / last_dice_roll, but no last_revealed_card). Omitting the life-loss clause per W5 is the right call. Commander ninjutsu is correctly dual-defined (Keyword marker line 28 + CommanderNinjutsu cost line 29); the Ninja-filtered combat damage trigger and the reveal-to-hand are implemented. |
| Zurgo and Ojutai | `zurgo_and_ojutai.rs` | `partial` | `keep` | Condition for 'entered the battlefield this turn' | Both stated gaps are real. (1) 'has hexproof as long as it entered this turn' needs a Condition testing the source's ETB turn; Condition's 48 variants contain nothing of the kind, and no Characteristics/GameObject field exposes an entered-this-turn timestamp to the layer system (has_summoning_sickness at game_object.rs:777 is close but is cleared by haste and is not a Condition-visible field тАФ using it would be wrong here anyway since this card HAS haste). (2) 'Whenever one or more Dragons you control deal combat damage to a player or battle' тАФ the batch variant TriggerEvent::AnyCreatureYouControlBatchCombatDamage exists, but the effect ('look at top three, put one into your hand, rest on the bottom in any order' + 'you may return one of those Dragons to its owner's hand') needs interactive selection, which Effect::Choose cannot express (effects/mod.rs:3190). Flying + haste are implemented (lines 20-21). |
